--- [Center Township, Clinton County, Iowa - Alchetron] ---
Elevation 196 m Local time Tuesday 9:26 AM | GNIS feature ID 0467572 Area 109.9 km² Population 626 (2000) | | Weather 6°C, Wind W at 40 km/h, 66% Humidity | Center Township is a township in Clinton County, Iowa, USA. At the 2000 census, its population was 626. Contents Map of Center, IA, USA History Center Township was organized in 1852. Geography Center Township covers an area of 42.42 square miles (109.9 km2) and contains no incorporated settlements. According to the USGS, it contains two cemeteries: Center Grove and Elvira.
